001|# Product Requirement Document for Web-Based Blackjack Game
002|
003|## 1. Language & Project Info
004|- **Language**: English
005|- **Programming Language**: React
006|- **Project Name**: web_based_blackjack_game
007|
008|## 2. Original Requirements
009|Create a web-based Blackjack game using modern HTML5 and JavaScript frameworks (React, Vue, etc.) for the front end and a secure backend for bet handling and session management, including an admin panel for table limits and player monitoring.
010|## 3. Product Goals
011|- **Goal 1**: Provide an engaging and interactive Blackjack gaming experience for users.
012|- **Goal 2**: Ensure secure and reliable bet handling and session management.
013|- **Goal 3**: Offer an intuitive admin panel for monitoring player activity and setting table limits.
014|
015|## 4. User Stories
016|- As a player, I want to easily join a game so that I can start playing quickly.
017|- As a player, I want to place bets securely so that I feel safe while playing.
018|- As an admin, I want to monitor player activity so that I can ensure fair play.
019|- As a player, I want to view my game history so that I can track my performance.
020|- As an admin, I want to set table limits so that I can manage the game effectively.
021|## 5. Competitive Analysis
022|- **Product A**: Online Blackjack Pro  
023|  - Pros: High-quality graphics, multiple game modes.  
024|  - Cons: Limited payment options.
025|
026|- **Product B**: Blackjack Royale  
027|  - Pros: User-friendly interface, mobile compatibility.  
028|  - Cons: Slow customer support.
029|
030|- **Product C**: Casino Blackjack  
031|  - Pros: Real-time multiplayer, engaging community features.  
032|  - Cons: High transaction fees.
033|
034|- **Product D**: Blackjack Master  
035|  - Pros: Comprehensive tutorials for beginners.  
036|  - Cons: Lacks advanced features for experienced players.
037|
038|- **Product E**: Virtual Blackjack  
039|  - Pros: Innovative betting options, frequent updates.  
040|  - Cons: Occasional bugs and glitches.
041|## 6. Technical Specifications
042|
043|### Requirements Analysis
044|- **Frontend**: Use React for building a responsive and interactive user interface.
045|- **Backend**: Implement a secure backend for handling bets and managing user sessions.
046|- **Database**: Use a reliable database for storing user data and game history.
047|- **Admin Panel**: Develop an admin panel for monitoring player activity and setting table limits.
048|
049|### Requirements Pool
050|- **P0**: Secure backend for bet handling and session management.
051|- **P1**: Responsive frontend using React.
052|- **P2**: Admin panel for player monitoring.
053|
054|### UI Design Draft
055|- The main game screen will display the Blackjack table, player cards, and betting options.
056|- The admin panel will include sections for player monitoring, table limits, and game statistics.
057|

059|- What specific security measures are required for the backend?
060|- Are there any specific design preferences for the UI?

011|- **Goal 1**: Provide an engaging and interactive Blackjack gaming experience for users.
012|- **Goal 2**: Ensure secure and reliable bet handling and session management.
013|- **Goal 3**: Offer an intuitive admin panel for monitoring player activity and setting table limits.
014|
015|## 4. User Stories
016|- As a player, I want to easily join a game so that I can start playing quickly.
017|- As a player, I want to place bets securely so that I feel safe while playing.
018|- As an admin, I want to monitor player activity so that I can ensure fair play.
019|- As a player, I want to view my game history so that I can track my performance.
020|- As an admin, I want to set table limits so that I can manage the game effectively.
021|## 5. Competitive Analysis
022|- **Product A**: Online Blackjack Pro  
023|  - Pros: High-quality graphics, multiple game modes.  
024|  - Cons: Limited payment options.
025|
026|- **Product B**: Blackjack Royale  
027|  - Pros: User-friendly interface, mobile compatibility.  
028|  - Cons: Slow customer support.
029|
030|- **Product C**: Casino Blackjack  
031|  - Pros: Real-time multiplayer, engaging community features.  
032|  - Cons: High transaction fees.
033|
034|- **Product D**: Blackjack Master  
035|  - Pros: Comprehensive tutorials for beginners.  
036|  - Cons: Lacks advanced features for experienced players.
037|
038|- **Product E**: Virtual Blackjack  
039|  - Pros: Innovative betting options, frequent updates.  
040|  - Cons: Occasional bugs and glitches.
041|## 6. Technical Specifications
042|
043|### Requirements Analysis
044|- **Frontend**: Use React for building a responsive and interactive user interface.
045|- **Backend**: Implement a secure backend for handling bets and managing user sessions.
046|- **Database**: Use a reliable database for storing user data and game history.
047|- **Admin Panel**: Develop an admin panel for monitoring player activity and setting table limits.
048|
049|### Requirements Pool
050|- **P0**: Secure backend for bet handling and session management.
051|- **P1**: Responsive frontend using React.
052|- **P2**: Admin panel for player monitoring.
053|
054|### UI Design Draft
055|- The main game screen will display the Blackjack table, player cards, and betting options.
056|- The admin panel will include sections for player monitoring, table limits, and game statistics.
